    Generic Debug

    name: datacenter, type: STRING
    name: vnfm-account-name, type: STRING
    name: sdn-account, type: STRING
    name: user-id, type: STRING, description: User who initiated the log event
    name: vnfr-id, type: STRING
    name: vnfr-name, type: STRING
    name: vnfd-id, type: STRING
    name: vnfd-name, type: STRING
    name: vnffgr-id, type: STRING
    name: vlr-id, type: STRING
    name: message, type: STRING

2.1.1.1  container nsr-log:template_params
  Leaves
    name: event-id, type: UINT32
    name: version, type: STRING
    name: sequence, type: UINT64
    name: sec, type: UINT32
    name: usec, type: UINT32
    name: system-id, type: STRING
    name: system-name, type: STRING
    name: hostname, type: STRING
    name: appname, type: STRING
    name: processid, type: UINT32
    name: threadid, type: UINT32
    name: filename, type: STRING
    name: linenumber, type: UINT32
    name: severity, type: ENUM
    name: crit-info, type: ENUM
    name: call-arrived-time, type: UINT32, description: Call arrived time
    name: call-failure, type: BOOLEAN, description: Call failure status
  XPath Path

  RW Keyspec XPath Path

2.1.1.1.3  container nsr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /nsr-log:generic-debug/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /nsr-log:generic-debug/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /nsr-log:generic-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/nsr-log:generic-debug/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/nsr-log:generic-debug/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .nsr_log.YangNotif.NsrLog.GenericDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    NsrLogYang.YangNotif_NsrLog_GenericDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    NsrLog__YangNotif__NsrLog__GenericDebug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_GenericDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    NsrLog_notif_GenericDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_GenericDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.4.1.3  container nsr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /nsr-log:generic-warning/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /nsr-log:generic-warning/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /nsr-log:generic-warning/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/nsr-log:generic-warning/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/nsr-log:generic-warning/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .nsr_log.YangNotif.NsrLog.GenericWarning.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    NsrLogYang.YangNotif_NsrLog_GenericWarning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    NsrLog__YangNotif__NsrLog__GenericWarning__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_GenericWarning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    NsrLog_notif_GenericWarning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

    rw_ypbc_NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_GenericWarning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.6.1.3  container nsr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /nsr-log:lookup-error/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /nsr-log:lookup-error/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /nsr-log:lookup-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/nsr-log:lookup-error/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/nsr-log:lookup-error/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .nsr_log.YangNotif.NsrLog.LookupError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    NsrLogYang.YangNotif_NsrLog_LookupError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    NsrLog__YangNotif__NsrLog__LookupError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_LookupError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    NsrLog_notif_LookupError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

    rw_ypbc_NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_LookupError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.9.1.3  container nsr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /nsr-log:scale-group-failure/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /nsr-log:scale-group-failure/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /nsr-log:scale-group-failure/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/nsr-log:scale-group-failure/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/nsr-log:scale-group-failure/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .nsr_log.YangNotif.NsrLog.ScaleGroupFailure.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    NsrLogYang.YangNotif_NsrLog_ScaleGroupFailure_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    NsrLog__YangNotif__NsrLog__ScaleGroupFailure__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_ScaleGroupFailure_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    NsrLog_notif_ScaleGroupFailure_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_ScaleGroupFailure_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.11.1.3  container nsr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /nsr-log:nsd-fetched/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /nsr-log:nsd-fetched/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /nsr-log:nsd-fetched/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/nsr-log:nsd-fetched/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/nsr-log:nsd-fetched/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .nsr_log.YangNotif.NsrLog.NsdFetched.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    NsrLogYang.YangNotif_NsrLog_NsdFetched_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    NsrLog__YangNotif__NsrLog__NsdFetched__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier

2.1.14.1.3  container nsr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /nsr-log:external-vl-instantiation-failed/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /nsr-log:external-vl-instantiation-failed/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /nsr-log:external-vl-instantiation-failed/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/nsr-log:external-vl-instantiation-failed/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/nsr-log:external-vl-instantiation-failed/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .nsr_log.YangNotif.NsrLog.ExternalVlInstantiationFailed.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    NsrLogYang.YangNotif_NsrLog_ExternalVlInstantiationFailed_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    NsrLog__YangNotif__NsrLog__ExternalVlInstantiationFailed__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_ExternalVlInstantiationFailed_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_ExternalVlInstantiationFailed_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.16.1.3  container nsr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /nsr-log:begin-vnf-instantiation/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /nsr-log:begin-vnf-instantiation/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /nsr-log:begin-vnf-instantiation/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/nsr-log:begin-vnf-instantiation/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/nsr-log:begin-vnf-instantiation/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .nsr_log.YangNotif.NsrLog.BeginVnfInstantiation.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    NsrLogYang.YangNotif_NsrLog_BeginVnfInstantiation_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    NsrLog__YangNotif__NsrLog__BeginVnfInstantiation__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_BeginVnfInstantiation_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    NsrLog_notif_BeginVnfInstantiation_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_BeginVnfInstantiation_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.19.1.3  container nsr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /nsr-log:vnf-scale-instantiated/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /nsr-log:vnf-scale-instantiated/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /nsr-log:vnf-scale-instantiated/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/nsr-log:vnf-scale-instantiated/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/nsr-log:vnf-scale-instantiated/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .nsr_log.YangNotif.NsrLog.VnfScaleInstantiated.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    NsrLogYang.YangNotif_NsrLog_VnfScaleInstantiated_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    NsrLog__YangNotif__NsrLog__VnfScaleInstantiated__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier

2.1.21.1.3  container nsr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /nsr-log:begin-vnffg-instantiation/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /nsr-log:begin-vnffg-instantiation/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /nsr-log:begin-vnffg-instantiation/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/nsr-log:begin-vnffg-instantiation/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/nsr-log:begin-vnffg-instantiation/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .nsr_log.YangNotif.NsrLog.BeginVnffgInstantiation.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    NsrLogYang.YangNotif_NsrLog_BeginVnffgInstantiation_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    NsrLog__YangNotif__NsrLog__BeginVnffgInstantiation__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_BeginVnffgInstantiation_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    NsrLog_notif_BeginVnffgInstantiation_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_BeginVnffgInstantiation_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.23.1.3  container nsr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /nsr-log:begin-scaling-group-instantiation/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /nsr-log:begin-scaling-group-instantiation/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /nsr-log:begin-scaling-group-instantiation/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/nsr-log:begin-scaling-group-instantiation/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/nsr-log:begin-scaling-group-instantiation/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .nsr_log.YangNotif.NsrLog.BeginScalingGroupInstantiation.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    NsrLogYang.YangNotif_NsrLog_BeginScalingGroupInstantiation_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    NsrLog__YangNotif__NsrLog__BeginScalingGroupInstantiation__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers

2.1.26.1.3  container nsr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /nsr-log:config-terminate/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /nsr-log:config-terminate/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /nsr-log:config-terminate/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/nsr-log:config-terminate/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/nsr-log:config-terminate/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .nsr_log.YangNotif.NsrLog.ConfigTerminate.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    NsrLogYang.YangNotif_NsrLog_ConfigTerminate_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    NsrLog__YangNotif__NsrLog__ConfigTerminate__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_ConfigTerminate_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    NsrLog_notif_ConfigTerminate_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_ConfigTerminate_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.28.1.3  container nsr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /nsr-log:nsd-not-found/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /nsr-log:nsd-not-found/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /nsr-log:nsd-not-found/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/nsr-log:nsd-not-found/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/nsr-log:nsd-not-found/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .nsr_log.YangNotif.NsrLog.NsdNotFound.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    NsrLogYang.YangNotif_NsrLog_NsdNotFound_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    NsrLog__YangNotif__NsrLog__NsdNotFound__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_NsdNotFound_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    NsrLog_notif_NsdNotFound_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.31.1.3  container nsr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /nsr-log:create-ns/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /nsr-log:create-ns/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /nsr-log:create-ns/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/nsr-log:create-ns/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/nsr-log:create-ns/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .nsr_log.YangNotif.NsrLog.CreateNs.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    NsrLogYang.YangNotif_NsrLog_CreateNs_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    NsrLog__YangNotif__NsrLog__CreateNs__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_CreateNs_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    NsrLog_notif_CreateNs_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_CreateNs_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

    rw_ypbc_NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_NsRunning_TemplateParams_AdditionalData

2.1.33.1.3  container nsr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /nsr-log:ns-running/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /nsr-log:ns-running/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /nsr-log:ns-running/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/nsr-log:ns-running/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/nsr-log:ns-running/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .nsr_log.YangNotif.NsrLog.NsRunning.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    NsrLogYang.YangNotif_NsrLog_NsRunning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    NsrLog__YangNotif__NsrLog__NsRunning__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_NsRunning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    NsrLog_notif_NsRunning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_NsRunning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.36.1.3  container nsr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /nsr-log:ns-instantiate-rpc/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /nsr-log:ns-instantiate-rpc/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /nsr-log:ns-instantiate-rpc/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/nsr-log:ns-instantiate-rpc/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/nsr-log:ns-instantiate-rpc/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .nsr_log.YangNotif.NsrLog.NsInstantiateRpc.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    NsrLogYang.YangNotif_NsrLog_NsInstantiateRpc_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    NsrLog__YangNotif__NsrLog__NsInstantiateRpc__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_NsInstantiateRpc_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    NsrLog_notif_NsInstantiateRpc_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_NsInstantiateRpc_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.38.1.3  container nsr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /nsr-log:ns-delete-rpc/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /nsr-log:ns-delete-rpc/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /nsr-log:ns-delete-rpc/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/nsr-log:ns-delete-rpc/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/nsr-log:ns-delete-rpc/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .nsr_log.YangNotif.NsrLog.NsDeleteRpc.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    NsrLogYang.YangNotif_NsrLog_NsDeleteRpc_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    NsrLog__YangNotif__NsrLog__NsDeleteRpc__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier

2.1.41.1.3  container nsr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /nsr-log:terminating-vnfs/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /nsr-log:terminating-vnfs/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /nsr-log:terminating-vnfs/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/nsr-log:terminating-vnfs/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/nsr-log:terminating-vnfs/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .nsr_log.YangNotif.NsrLog.TerminatingVnfs.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    NsrLogYang.YangNotif_NsrLog_TerminatingVnfs_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    NsrLog__YangNotif__NsrLog__TerminatingVnfs__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_TerminatingVnfs_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    NsrLog_notif_TerminatingVnfs_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_TerminatingVnfs_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.43.1.3  container nsr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /nsr-log:ns-terminated/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /nsr-log:ns-terminated/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /nsr-log:ns-terminated/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/nsr-log:ns-terminated/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/nsr-log:ns-terminated/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .nsr_log.YangNotif.NsrLog.NsTerminated.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    NsrLogYang.YangNotif_NsrLog_NsTerminated_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    NsrLog__YangNotif__NsrLog__NsTerminated__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier

2.1.46.1.3  container nsr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /nsr-log:terminate-rcvd/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /nsr-log:terminate-rcvd/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /nsr-log:terminate-rcvd/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/nsr-log:terminate-rcvd/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/nsr-log:terminate-rcvd/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .nsr_log.YangNotif.NsrLog.TerminateRcvd.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    NsrLogYang.YangNotif_NsrLog_TerminateRcvd_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    NsrLog__YangNotif__NsrLog__TerminateRcvd__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_TerminateRcvd_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.48.1.3  container nsr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /nsr-log:rollback-rcvd/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /nsr-log:rollback-rcvd/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /nsr-log:rollback-rcvd/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/nsr-log:rollback-rcvd/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/nsr-log:rollback-rcvd/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .nsr_log.YangNotif.NsrLog.RollbackRcvd.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    NsrLogYang.YangNotif_NsrLog_RollbackRcvd_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

    NsrLog__YangNotif__NsrLog__RollbackRcvd__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier

2.1.51.1.3  container nsr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /nsr-log:datastore-event/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /nsr-log:datastore-event/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /nsr-log:datastore-event/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/nsr-log:datastore-event/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/nsr-log:datastore-event/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .nsr_log.YangNotif.NsrLog.DatastoreEvent.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    NsrLogYang.YangNotif_NsrLog_DatastoreEvent_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    NsrLog__YangNotif__NsrLog__DatastoreEvent__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_DatastoreEvent_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    NsrLog_notif_DatastoreEvent_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_DatastoreEvent_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.56.1.3  container nsr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /nsr-log:async-operation-failed/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /nsr-log:async-operation-failed/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /nsr-log:async-operation-failed/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/nsr-log:async-operation-failed/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/nsr-log:async-operation-failed/nsr-log:template_params/nsr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .nsr_log.YangNotif.NsrLog.AsyncOperationFailed.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    NsrLogYang.YangNotif_NsrLog_AsyncOperationFailed_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    NsrLog__YangNotif__NsrLog__AsyncOperationFailed__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_AsyncOperationFailed_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    NsrLog_notif_AsyncOperationFailed_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_NsrLog_NsrLog_notif_AsyncOperationFailed_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
